\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em -\/1} & Indications the device shall never use the I\+MS A\+PN for R\+CS. \\
\hline
{\em 0} & Indications The device shall use the I\+MS A\+PN for R\+CS when the device\textquotesingle{}s internet access is using cellular coverage. \\
\hline
{\em 1} & Indications the device shall always use the I\+MS A\+PN for R\+CS whenever it is in cellular coverage, even if non-\/cellular access is available.\\

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Z\+F\+U\+NC Z\+B\+O\+OL Mtc\+\_\+\+Cli\+Db\+Get\+Rcs\+Disable\+State (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get rcs disable state. 


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em 1,the} & client is rcs enable. \\
\hline
{\em 0,the} & client is temporarily disabled. \\
\hline
{\em -\/1,the} & client is permanently disabled. \\
\hline
{\em -\/2,the} & client is permanently disabled, but user triggered events result in an attempt to re-\/enable the client. \\
\hline
{\em -\/3,the} & client is placed in dormant state.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
